### [121] [From Spark to Fire: Modeling and Mitigating Error Cascades in LLM-Based Multi-Agent Collaboration](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04474)
*Yizhe Xie,Congcong Zhu,Xinyue Zhang,Tianqing Zhu,Dayong Ye,Minfeng Qi,Huajie Chen,Wanlei Zhou*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 该论文研究了大语言模型多智能体系统中错误传播与放大的风险，提出了传播动力学模型识别三类安全漏洞，并通过系谱图治理层将防御成功率从32%提升至89%以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM-MAS在复杂协作场景中应用广泛，但其协作机制可能导致微小不准确在迭代中逐渐固化为系统级错误共识，且错误可通过消息依赖传播和放大。现有保护方案依赖单智能体验证或需修改协作架构，可能削弱有效信息流。

Method: 1) 建立LLM-MAS的传播动力学模型，将协作抽象为有向依赖图并提供早期风险标准；2) 在六个主流框架上进行实验，识别三类漏洞（级联放大、拓扑敏感性、共识惯性）；3) 实施单原子错误种子注入攻击验证漏洞；4) 引入系谱图治理层作为消息层插件防御。

Result: 1) 识别三类漏洞：级联放大、拓扑敏感性和共识惯性；2) 仅注入单个原子错误种子即可导致广泛失败；3) 防御成功率从0.32提升至0.89以上，显著缓解级联传播。

Conclusion: 该研究提出了基于系谱图的治理层，作为消息层插件实现，可在不改变协作架构的情况下抑制内源性和外源性错误放大，将防御成功率从0.32提升至0.89以上，显著减轻了微小错误的级联传播。

Abstract: Large Language Model-based Multi-Agent Systems (LLM-MAS) are increasingly applied to complex collaborative scenarios. However, their collaborative mechanisms may cause minor inaccuracies to gradually solidify into system-level false consensus through iteration. Such risks are difficult to trace since errors can propagate and amplify through message dependencies. Existing protections often rely on single-agent validation or require modifications to the collaboration architecture, which can weaken effective information flow and may not align with natural collaboration processes in real tasks. To address this, we propose a propagation dynamics model tailored for LLM-MAS that abstracts collaboration as a directed dependency graph and provides an early-stage risk criterion to characterize amplification risk. Through experiments on six mainstream frameworks, we identify three vulnerability classes: cascade amplification, topological sensitivity, and consensus inertia. We further instantiate an attack where injecting just a single atomic error seed leads to widespread failure. In response, we introduce a genealogy-graph-based governance layer, implemented as a message-layer plugin, that suppresses both endogenous and exogenous error amplification without altering the collaboration architecture. Experiments show that this approach raises the defense success rate from a baseline of 0.32 to over 0.89 and significantly mitigates the cascading spread of minor errors.

</details>


### [122] [Strategic Interactions in Multi-Level Stackelberg Games with Non-Follower Agents and Heterogeneous Leaders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04628)
*Niloofar Aminikalibar,Farzaneh Farhadi,Maria Chli*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: 本文针对现有Stackelberg拥堵模型忽略非跟随者智能体的问题，提出三层Stackelberg博弈框架，通过引入异质性领导者、战略性跟随者和非跟随者，捕捉基础设施决策、竞争与均衡拥堵之间的双向耦合，并以电动汽车充电基础设施为例验证了该框架的适用性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型通常忽略不直接参与市场竞争但同样贡献并适应拥堵的非跟随者智能体，其行为虽然不产生收入或响应市场激励，但会重塑拥堵模式，进而通过共享资源影响领导者和跟随者的决策。忽视非跟随者导致拥堵耦合市场中的均衡预测出现系统性扭曲。

Method: 构建了一个三层Stackelberg博弈框架，包含异质性领导者（不同决策视野和可行行动）、战略性跟随者以及非跟随者智能体，并将其具体应用于电动汽车充电基础设施场景进行验证。

Result: 模型表明，明确考虑非跟随者和异质性竞争者会定性地改变战略激励和均衡结果，揭示了传统模型无法捕捉的关键动态特征。

Conclusion: 该框架可应用于移动、能源和计算市场中更广泛的拥堵耦合多智能体系统，为理解和优化涉及非跟随者的复杂竞争环境提供了新范式。

Abstract: Strategic interaction in congested systems is commonly modelled using Stackelberg games, where competing leaders anticipate the behaviour of self-interested followers. A key limitation of existing models is that they typically ignore agents who do not directly participate in market competition, yet both contribute to and adapt to congestion. Although such non-follower agents do not generate revenue or respond to market incentives, their behaviour reshapes congestion patterns, which in turn affects the decisions of leaders and followers through shared resources.
  We argue that overlooking non-followers leads to systematically distorted equilibrium predictions in congestion-coupled markets. To address this, we introduce a three-level Stackelberg framework with heterogeneous leaders differing in decision horizons and feasible actions, strategic followers, and non-follower agents that captures bidirectional coupling between infrastructure decisions, competition, and equilibrium congestion.
  We instantiate the framework in the context of electric vehicle (EV) charging infrastructure, where charging providers compete with rivals, while EV and non-EV traffic jointly shape congestion. The model illustrates how explicitly accounting for non-followers and heterogeneous competitors qualitatively alters strategic incentives and equilibrium outcomes. Beyond EV charging, the framework applies to a broad class of congestion-coupled multi-agent systems in mobility, energy, and computing markets.

### [123] [SCoUT: Scalable Communication via Utility-Guided Temporal Grouping in Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04833)
*Manav Vora,Gokul Puthumanaillam,Hiroyasu Tsukamoto,Melkior Ornik*

Main category: cs.MA

TL;DR: SCoUT通过时间分组和智能体抽象解决部分可观测多智能体强化学习中的通信学习问题，使用Gumbel-Softmax进行软分组，引入组感知评论家和反事实通信优势实现精确信用分配，最终实现去中心化执行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在部分可观测的多智能体强化学习中，学习何时以及与谁通信面临两个挑战：1) 需要在众多可能的发送者-接收者对中选择；2) 难以隔离单条信息对未来奖励的影响。

Method: 1) 时间抽象：每K个环境步骤通过Gumbel-Softmax重采样软智能体组作为潜在线索；2) 智能体抽象：利用分组亲和力作为可微分的接收者先验；3) 组感知评论家：预测每组价值并通过软分配映射到智能体基线；4) 三头策略：环境动作、发送决策、接收者选择；5) 反事实通信优势：通过解析移除发送者贡献实现精确信用分配。

Result: 降低了评论家复杂度和方差，实现了发送和接收者选择的精确信用分配，训练时保留所有集中组件，执行时仅运行智能体策略保持去中心化执行。

Conclusion: SCoUT为MARL中的通信学习提供了一种可扩展的解决方案，通过时间分组和反事实推理有效解决了通信学习的计算效率和信用分配问题。]

Abstract: Communication can improve coordination in partially observed multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL), but learning \emph{when} and \emph{who} to communicate with requires choosing among many possible sender-recipient pairs, and the effect of any single message on future reward is hard to isolate. We introduce \textbf{SCoUT} (\textbf{S}calable \textbf{Co}mmunication via \textbf{U}tility-guided \textbf{T}emporal grouping), which addresses both these challenges via temporal and agent abstraction within traditional MARL. During training, SCoUT resamples \textit{soft} agent groups every \(K\) environment steps (macro-steps) via Gumbel-Softmax; these groups are latent clusters that induce an affinity used as a differentiable prior over recipients. Using the same assignments, a group-aware critic predicts values for each agent group and maps them to per-agent baselines through the same soft assignments, reducing critic complexity and variance. Each agent is trained with a three-headed policy: environment action, send decision, and recipient selection. To obtain precise communication learning signals, we derive counterfactual communication advantages by analytically removing each sender's contribution from the recipient's aggregated messages. This counterfactual computation enables precise credit assignment for both send and recipient-selection decisions. At execution time, all centralized training components are discarded and only the per-agent policy is run, preserving decentralized execution. Project website, videos and code: \hyperlink{https://scout-comm.github.io/}{https://scout-comm.github.io/}

</details>

### [124] [Hypercube drawings with no long plane paths](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04665)
*Todor Antić,Niloufar Fuladi,Anna Margarethe Limbach,Pavel Valtr*

Main category: cs.CG

TL;DR: 研究d维超立方体图Q_d在各种绘制中的平面子结构性质，给出了平面子图、路径和匹配的大小上界，证明了凸位置直线绘制中必然存在指定长度的平面路径，并确定了大d时不变平面子图的结构特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究超立方体图Q_d的绘制中平面子结构的存在性问题，探讨在各种绘制方式下能够获得的平面子图、平面路径和平面匹配的大小上界。

Method: 通过构造特殊绘制和证明存在性定理两种方法，运用了极值图论和几何图论的技术手段。

Result: 构造了没有超过2d-2条边的平面子图、没有超过2d-3条边的平面路径、没有超过2d-4条边的平面匹配的Q_d绘制；证明了凸位置直线绘制中包含长度为d或d-1的平面路径；证明了平面子图必然是毛毛虫森林；推广了直线交叉数结果。

Conclusion: 证明了在超立方体图的绘制中，平面子结构的存在性受到显著限制，并且给出了任意Q_d的直线绘制中必然存在的平面路径长度，同时证明了如果图G是所有充分大d的Q_d的绘制的平面子图，则G必须是毛毛虫森林，最后给出了直线交叉数结果的推广证明。

Abstract: We study the existence of plane substructures in drawings of the $d$-dimensional hypercube graph $Q_d$. We construct drawings of $Q_d$ which contain no plane subgraph with more than $2d-2$ edges, no plane path with more than $2d-3$ edges, and no plane matching of size more than $2d-4$. On the other hand, we prove that every rectilinear drawing of $Q_d$ with vertices in convex position contains a plane path of length $d$ (if $d$ is odd) or $d-1$ (if $d$ is even). We also prove that if a graph $G$ is a plane subgraph of every drawing of $Q_d$ for a sufficiently large $d$, then $G$ is necessarily a forest of caterpillars. Lastly, we give a short proof of a generalization of a result by Alpert et al. [Cong. Numerantium, 2009] on the maximum rectilinear crossing number of $Q_d$.

</details>


### [125] [Quadratic polarity and polar Fenchel-Young divergences from the canonical Legendre polarity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04812)
*Frank Nielsen,Basile Plus-Gourdon,Mahito Sugiyama*

Main category: cs.CG

TL;DR: 本文研究n维射影几何中极性(polarity)的基本理论及其与信息几何中Legendre-Fenchel变换的联系，提出极性散度(polar divergences)的概念，推广了Fenchel-Young散度和Bregman散度，并揭示了信息几何中的参考对偶性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极性是n维射影几何中的基本互惠对偶性，将点与极超平面相关联。Legendre-Fenchel变换可以从极性视角通过添加额外维度来解释。然而，如何系统性地理解和操作这些极性变换，以及它们在信息几何中的更深层应用此前尚未被充分探索。

Method: 首先，证明由二次极性泛函诱导的通用极性可以表示为变形Legendre极性或变形凸体的Legendre极性，并利用(n+2)×(n+2)矩阵上的线性代数在齐次坐标上高效操作。其次，定义基于Legendre极性的极性散度，证明其推广了Fenchel-Young散度或等价的Bregman散度。最后，证明总Bregman散度可视为总极性Fenchel-Young散度，并利用对偶极性共形因子展示参考对偶性。

Result: 通用极性可以通过(n+2)×(n+2)矩阵的线性代数高效处理和表示。极性散度成功推广了Fenchel-Young散度和Bregman散度。总Bregman散度可以被理解为总极性Fenchel-Young散度，从而揭示了参考对偶性的新表现形式。

Conclusion: 极性研究为信息几何中的核心参考对偶性提供了新的理解视角，建立了射影几何极性与信息几何散度理论之间的深刻联系，为进一步研究对偶性结构铺平了道路。

Abstract: Polarity is a fundamental reciprocal duality of $n$-dimensional projective geometry which associates to points polar hyperplanes, and more generally $k$-dimensional convex bodies to polar $(n-1-k)$-dimensional convex bodies. It is well-known that the Legendre-Fenchel transformation of functions can be interpreted from the polarity viewpoint of their graphs using an extra dimension. In this paper, we first show that generic polarities induced by quadratic polarity functionals can be expressed either as deformed Legendre polarity or as the Legendre polarity of deformed convex bodies, and be efficiently manipulated using linear algebra on $(n+2)\times (n+2)$ matrices operating on homogeneous coordinates. Second, we define polar divergences using the Legendre polarity and show that they generalize the Fenchel-Young divergence or equivalent Bregman divergence. This polarity study brings new understanding of the core reference duality in information geometry. Last, we show that the total Bregman divergences can be considered as a total polar Fenchel-Young divergence from which we newly exhibit the reference duality using dual polar conformal factors.

</details>


### [126] [An Optimal Algorithm for Computing Many Faces in Line Arrangements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.04863)
*Haitao Wang*

Main category: cs.CG

TL;DR: 给定平面上的m个点和n条直线，计算包含至少一个点的直线排列面的问题，首个最优算法实现O(m^{2/3}n^{2/3}+(n+m)log n)时间复杂度，在m=n时达到O(n^{4/3})，匹配输出组合复杂度下界


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该问题自1988年Edelsbrunner等人首次研究以来，一直未能找到最优算法，因此需要找到一个在代数决策树模型下的最优算法

Method: 提出了一种时间复杂度为O(m^{2/3}n^{2/3}+(n+m)log n)的算法

Result: 算法的时间复杂度为O(m^{2/3}n^{2/3}+(n+m)log n)，当m=n时为O(n^{4/3})，与输出面数的组合复杂度下界Ω(n^{4/3})相匹配

Conclusion: 该算法在代数决策树模型下达到最优，解决了近35年来未解决的最优性问题。当m=n时，运行时间为O(n^{4/3})，与输出面数的组合复杂度下界Ω(n^{4/3})相匹配。

Abstract: Given a set of $m$ points and a set of $n$ lines in the plane, we consider the problem of computing the faces of the arrangement of the lines that contain at least one point. In this paper, we present an $O(m^{2/3}n^{2/3}+(n+m)\log n)$ time algorithm for the problem. We also show that this matches the lower bound under the algebraic decision tree model and thus our algorithm is optimal. In particular, when $m=n$, the runtime is $O(n^{4/3})$, which matches the worst case combinatorial complexity $Ω(n^{4/3})$ of all output faces. This is the first optimal algorithm since the problem was first studied more than three decades ago [Edelsbrunner, Guibas, and Sharir, SoCG 1988].

</details>


### [127] [Structural Properties of Shortest Flip Sequences Between Plane Spanning Trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05205)
*Oswin Aichholzer,Joseph Dorfer,Peter Kramer,Christian Rieck,Birgit Vogtenhuber*

Main category: cs.CG

TL;DR: 研究凸位置上点集平面生成树的重构问题，分析最短翻转序列的结构特性，探讨三个相关猜想的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平面生成树重构是计算几何中的基础问题。研究者提出三个重要猜想：快乐边猜想（初始和目标树共享的边不应被翻转）、停车边猜想（存在只使用初始树、目标树和凸包边的最短翻转序列）、重新停车猜想（任何边翻转不超过两次）。这些猜想被广泛用于flip算法，但缺乏严格证明。

Method: 研究最短翻转序列的结构特性，通过构造反例和分析特定情况下的行为，检验三个猜想在一般情况和特殊案例中的有效性。

Result: 发现停车边猜想和重新停车猜想在某些情况下成立，但在一般设置下不成立，成功反驳了这两个猜想。快乐边猜想未被直接反驳。

Conclusion: 三个猜想并非普遍成立，研究者确定了某些情况下猜想成立的条件，并给出了一般情况下的反例。这为平面生成树重构领域提供了重要的理论贡献，澄清了这些猜想的适用范围。

Abstract: We study the reconfiguration of plane spanning trees on point sets in the plane in convex position, where a reconfiguration step (flip) replaces one edge with another, yielding again a plane spanning tree. The flip distance between two trees is then the minimum number of flips needed to transform one tree into the other. We study structural properties of shortest flip sequences.
  The folklore happy edge conjecture suggests that any edge shared by both the initial and target tree is never flipped in a shortest flip sequence. The more recent parking edge conjecture, which would have implied the happy edge conjecture, states that there exist shortest flip sequences which use only edges of the start and target tree, and edges in the convex hull of the point set. Finally, another conjecture that is implicit in the literature is the reparking conjecture which states that no edge is flipped more than twice. Essentially all recent flip algorithms respect these three conjectures and the properties they imply. We study cases in which the latter two conjectures hold and disprove them for the general setting.
  (Shortened abstract due to arXiv restrictions.)

</details>


### [128] [What induces plane structures in complete graph drawings?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05208)
*Alexandra Weinberger,Ji Zeng*

Main category: cs.CG

TL;DR: 研究完整图中曲线绘制问题，证明了在特定规则下不可避免地会出现多条互不相交曲线，并给出了无不相交曲线的构造方法


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究在纸上连接点对之间的曲线绘制问题，探讨在不同规则下曲线相交和不相交的特性

Method: 通过拓扑图论方法，分析完整图绘制中曲线的相交模式

Result: 证明了在温和假设下，若满足邻接曲线不相交或非邻接曲线最多相交一次的规则，则必然存在多条互不相交的曲线；同时构造出一种绘制方式使邻接曲线恰好相交一次，非邻接曲线至少相交一次至多两次，且无不相交曲线

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了图绘制中相交模式的深刻性质，分类刻画了不同规则下保证的平面结构，为拓扑图论提供了新的理论贡献

Abstract: This paper considers the task of connecting points on a piece of paper by drawing a curve between each pair of them. Under mild assumptions, we prove that many pairwise disjoint curves are unavoidable if either of the following rules is obeyed: any two adjacent curves do not cross, or any two non-adjacent curves cross at most once. Here, two curves are called adjacent if they share an endpoint. On the other hand, we demonstrate how to draw all curves such that any two adjacent curves cross exactly once, any two non-adjacent curves cross at least once and at most twice, and thus no two curves are disjoint. Furthermore, we analyze the emergence of disjoint curves without these mild assumptions, and characterize the plane structures in complete graph drawings guaranteed by each of the rules above.

</details>


### [129] [Drone Air Traffic Control: Tracking a Set of Moving Objects with Minimal Power](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05286)

TL;DR: 本文研究如何调整 stationary traffic control stations 的传感范围来监控移动设备，以优化能耗。即使所有物体沿直线匀速运动，也无法在多项式时间内获得最优覆盖，但基于几何洞察的算法可在秒级时间内处理500个移动物体和25个站点的实例，展示出实时能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 理论方面证明即使所有物体沿直线匀速运动，也无法在多项式时间内获得最优解。实践方面提出基于几何洞察的算法来解决min-max变体问题。

Result: 该算法能够处理500个移动物体和25个站点，运行时长仅需数秒，展示了实时处理能力。

Conclusion: 虽然理论上存在计算复杂性挑战，但基于几何方法的算法在实际应用中表现出色，能够满足实时需求。

Abstract: A common sensing problem is to use a set of stationary tracking locations to monitor a collection of moving devices: Given $n$ objects that need to be tracked, each following its own trajectory, and $m$ stationary traffic control stations, each with a sensing region of adjustable range; how should we adjust the individual sensor ranges in order to optimize energy consumption? We provide both negative theoretical and positive practical results for this important and natural challenge.
  On the theoretical side, we show that even if all objects move at constant speed along straight lines, no polynomial-time algorithm can guarantee optimal coverage for a given starting solution. On the practical side, we present an algorithm based on geometric insights that is able to find optimal solutions for the $\min \max$ variant of the problem, which aims at minimizing peak power consumption. Runtimes for instances with 500 moving objects and 25 stations are in the order of seconds for scenarios that take minutes to play out in the real world, demonstrating real-time capability of our methods.

Abstract: We consider colored variants of a class of geometric-combinatorial questions on $k$-gons and empty $k$-gons that have been started around 1935 by Erdős and Szekeres. In our setting we have $n$ points in general position in the plane, each one colored either red or blue. A structure on $k$ points is a geometric graph where the edges are spanned by (some of) these points and is called monochromatic if all $k$ points have the same color. Already for $k=4$ there exist interesting open problems. Most prominently, it is still open whether for any sufficiently large bichromatic set there always exists a convex empty, monochromatic quadrilateral. In order to shed more light on the underlying geometry we study the existence of five different monochromatic structures that all use exactly 4 points of a bichromatic point set. We provide several improved lower and upper bounds on the smallest $n$ such that every bichromatic set of at least $n$ points contains (some of) those monochromatic structures.

### [131] [Revisiting Graph Modification via Disk Scaling: From One Radius to Interval-Based Radii](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05358)
*Thomas Depian,Frank Sommer*

Main category: cs.CG

TL;DR: This paper generalizes disk scaling for unit disk graphs by allowing flexible radii within an interval. It establishes XP membership for recognizable graph classes, proves NP-hardness but FPT for cluster graphs, polynomial-time for complete graphs, and W[1]-hardness for connected graphs, answering open questions from prior work.


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: The paper addresses a gap in graph modification problems for geometric graphs. While classic operations like vertex/edge deletions don't consider geometric properties, this work generalizes the disk scaling operation from Fomin et al. (ITCS'25). The key innovation is allowing disks to have flexible radii within an interval [r_min, r_max] rather than a fixed radius, which makes the model more practical for real-world applications.

Method: The authors study the parameterized complexity of Π-Scaling with respect to k (the number of modifications). They prove membership in XP for polynomial-time recognizable graph classes, and analyze complexity for specific graph classes: cluster graphs, complete graphs, and connected graphs.

Result: The main results include: (1) Π-Scaling is in XP for any polynomial-time recognizable graph class; (2) NP-hard but FPT for cluster graphs; (3) polynomial-time solvable for complete graphs; (4) W[1]-hard for connected graphs.

Conclusion: This work answers open questions from Fomin et al. and provides a comprehensive complexity analysis of the generalized disk scaling problem. The W[1]-hardness result for connected graphs generalizes the hardness result for restricted disk sets. The work establishes the boundaries between tractable and intractable cases in this new geometric graph modification framework.

Abstract: For a fixed graph class $Π$, the goal of $Π$-Modification is to transform an input graph $G$ into a graph $H\inΠ$ using at most $k$ modifications. Vertex and edge deletions are common operations, and their (parameterized) complexity for various $Π$ is well-studied. Classic graph modification operations such as edge deletion do not consider the geometric nature of geometric graphs such as (unit) disk graphs. This led Fomin et al. [ITCS' 25] to initiate the study of disk scaling as a geometric graph modification operation for unit disk graphs: For a given radius $r$, each modified disk will be rescaled to radius $r$. In this paper, we generalize their model by allowing rescaled disks to choose a radius within a given interval $[r_{\min}, r_{\max}]$ and study the (parameterized) complexity (with respect to $k$) of the corresponding problem $Π$-Scaling. We show that $Π$-Scaling is in XP for every graph class $Π$ that can be recognized in polynomial time. Furthermore, we show that $Π$-Scaling: (1) is NP-hard and FPT for cluster graphs, (2) can be solved in polynomial time for complete graphs, and (3) is W[1]-hard for connected graphs. In particular, (1) and (2) answer open questions of Fomin et al. and (3) generalizes the hardness result for their variant where the set of scalable disks is restricted.

</details>


### [132] [ETH-Tight Complexity of Optimal Morse Matching on Bounded-Treewidth Complexes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.05406)
*Geevarghese Philip,Erlend Raa Vågset*

Main category: cs.CG

TL;DR: 研究最优Morse匹配(OMM)问题的参数化复杂度，解决了一个长期开放问题。给出树宽参数k下2^{O(k log k)} n时间算法，并证明该算法在ETH下是最优的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OMM问题是NP难问题，长期以来在参数化复杂性方面有研究。之前已知在树宽k参数下，3-流形三角剖分可在2^{O(k^2)} n^{O(1)}时间内解决，但对于任意流形三角剖分只有FPT时间结果，k的精确依赖关系一直未知。本文旨在解决这个开放问题。

Method: 本文采用新的算法设计技术，针对有限正则CW复形设计算法。证明下界时利用ETH假设，通过从3-SAT问题归约来证明不存在更快的算法。

Result: 给出任意有限正则CW复形的OMM问题的2^{O(k log k)} n时间算法，并证明在ETH假设下不存在2^{o(k log k)} n^{O(1)}时间算法。

Conclusion: 给出了任意有限正则CW复形的2^{O(k log k)} n时间算法，并证明在ETH假设下不存在2^{o(k log k)} n^{O(1)}时间算法，从而解决了OMM问题在树宽参数下的精确复杂度问题。该算法相比之前的2^{O(k^2)} n^{O(1)}时间有了显著改进。

Abstract: The Optimal Morse Matching (OMM) problem asks for a discrete gradient vector field on a simplicial complex that minimizes the number of critical simplices. It is NP-hard and has been studied extensively in heuristic, approximation, and parameterized complexity settings. Parameterized by treewidth $k$, OMM has long been known to be solvable on triangulations of $3$-manifolds in $2^{O(k^2)} n^{O(1)}$ time and in FPT time for triangulations of arbitrary manifolds, but the exact dependence on $k$ has remained an open question. We resolve this by giving a new $2^{O(k \log k)} n$-time algorithm for any finite regular CW complex, and show that no $2^{o(k \log k)} n^{O(1)}$-time algorithm exists unless the Exponential Time Hypothesis (ETH) fails.

</details>
